msg:Although it is an old hotel with a few years of history, the hotel has been renovated and looks brand new. It does not feel old, and the accommodation experience meets the standards of a five-star hotel. The hotel is in a unique location. After getting off the plane, take the airport east line to the terminal "Golden Bay Hotel", which is diagonally opposite. Xingyuan Food Street is on the right side of the hotel. There are many food stores recommended by "Dianping" on the street. Hotel guests who do not include breakfast can easily solve their breakfast in the teahouse on the street. Cantonese-style morning tea is famous all over the world and is worth tasting. Not far from the hotel is the famous Longyan South Road Food Street. The liveliness of this street is amazing. The hotel's swimming pool is beautiful, clean, and spacious. The service staff is also very warm and friendly. It is really friendly to travelers who like swimming. If you are full in the food street, go to the beautiful swimming pool for a swim. Don't be too comfortable. Taste the food and swim in the swimming pool every day. Living in Junhua really feels like a mouse falling into a rice jar.
The most impressive thing about the hotel is the high-quality service, which must be praised as the last point. I received a call from the housekeeper Ruby Hwang the day before I checked in, asking if I had any needs for the hotel. When I arrived at the hotel, I saw the welcome fruits and small gifts in bags, which made me feel very kind and warm. During my stay, Ruby asked about my well-being every day, which made me feel at home. Thank you for her excellent service and thank you for your hard work.
In addition to the excellent housekeeper service, the front desk staff are also polite and well-trained. Every problem encountered can always be solved quickly by them. Junhua's management level is excellent, absolutely five-star 10 level.
The aunt who cleans the room is serious and careful. The room is cleaned very cleanly. When she sees the guests, she will take the initiative to greet them kindly. It can be seen that she has received good training. I would like to take this opportunity to praise the cleaning aunt Helen and Alice in the room. Thank you for your hard work.
This Shantou food tour is really worth it. We have a good stay, good food, and a good mood. Among them, staying in Junhua Haiyi is our most correct choice.
Travelers, do you want to experience the feeling of home during your trip? When you come to Shantou, don't hesitate. Choosing Junhua Haiyi is absolutely right.

It is an old five-star hotel, and the environment is definitely not bad. The lobby is spacious and grand. The room is also spacious. The facilities are definitely not as new as those in new hotels, but they are not as old as some comments. The wooden furniture is better in terms of heritage.
There is a dressing table and a makeup mirror, which is amazing.
I was quite satisfied at first, but I didn’t know that when I went to bed in the early morning, the KTV downstairs would sing until midnight. It was too noisy. For a light sleeper like me, it was very depressing. I originally wanted to change a hotel the next day. The staff member Zhang Yongfang explained carefully and decisively to change our room. rating:5
posted:Posted March 20, 2023
msg:I took the elderly and children to travel to Chaoshan together, and I struggled with the accommodation issue in Shantou for a long time. I wanted to stay at the Sheraton or the International Hotel, but after reading the reviews, my heart beat. In addition, the Sheraton and the International Hotel were basically fully booked during the first few days of March. Let’s talk about the disadvantages first, what is said on the Internet is true, the hotel has been renovated for a long time, and the decoration and facilities do have a sense of age, but overall it still has the temperament of an old five-star hotel. Although the decoration of the facilities is old, the maintenance is relatively good. Let’s talk about the advantages. The service of the hotel is very good. From the front desk to the restaurant to the guest room, the service staff are polite and enthusiastic. The bellman in the lobby (I forgot to ask the name, he is from Lanzhou) gave us sufficient introduction and guidance. He gave us a lot of travel and food strategies and suggestions, and gave the child a box of gifts similar to Barbie dolls. The child liked it very much. The breakfast in the hotel is also very good. There are Western-style breakfasts and local specialties. I ate rice rolls and kway teow for two days after staying for two days. Haha, it tastes great. The hotel has a free underground parking lot, and there is a swimming pool on the fourth floor, where children swim every day. The location of the hotel is also very good, not far from Longyan South Road. If you want to eat snacks at night, you can walk there. Although it is facing the street, the room is on a high floor and not noisy. All in all, this stay is very satisfying.

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r

msg:作為老牌星級酒店，這家酒店的總體衞生和服務絕對沒得説，地處中心，附近很多美食和購物，而且在週末，房價是五百左右一晚絕對算得上是性價比超高！！！

美中不足的是，浴缸還有一點污漬，最後還是我自己洗乾淨了才敢泡澡的，衞生細緻方面有待加強。另外作為老牌酒店，設施先進性方面相比其他近年來的新酒店較落後，比如電視機不夠智能、外賣配送也不夠方便（衹能送到門口外賣櫃然後打電話讓禮賓服務送上來），房間裏面的插座也不夠多（比如衞生間裏竟然沒有插頭），但這些可以理解，畢竟年份擺在那裡了。

總體來説，出遊住老牌酒店還是很安心，值得推薦給來汕頭旅遊的朋友們～^_^

總結：4-5星級的大堂和樓層走道，3星級的房間。如果不是睡覺我都想在大堂待久一點，不想上樓聞廁所味...

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Selected Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in February 2023
info:Couples
info:4 Reviews
rating:4.2
posted:Posted March 3, 2023
msg:位置十分便利，應該是當地的老五星級酒店了。入住當日發現書桌前標註“不間斷”電源的插座沒有電，其餘除去靠窗牀頭櫃有一個酒店提供的魔方插座，再無可用電源，其餘所有電源都是英標！！！電視、電水壺的電線都被重新接的英標插頭。（所以是港商早年的酒店？）早説帶上我英標的轉換插頭啊！報修後第二天插座修好，維修態度很好。

再説説空調，衹有製冷，沒有暖風，在降温的幾天裏晚上有些涼，可以忍受。但沒有空調屋裡會非常非常潮，打開空調又實在冷。

淋浴設施可以用簡陋來形容，想起了大學澡堂裏那歪歪扭扭的蓮蓬頭。

早飯簡單，有現煮湯粉或粿條，中規中矩。但也不像很多五星酒店可以用“豐盛”來形容。湊合吃吃沒有問題。

整體感覺心理建設上，用老四星水準迎接這家酒店可能更合適一些。現在新的三星級標準酒店甚至連鎖商旅酒店硬件可能都要比這個好了。
